2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Remote GitHub MCP server has optional headers equivalent to the Local server env vars or flags:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eX-MCP-Toolsets\u003c/code\u003e: Comma-separated list of toolsets to enable. E.g. \"repos,issues\".\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEquivalent to \u003ccode\u003eGITHUB_TOOLSETS\u003c/code\u003e env var or \u003ccode\u003e--toolsets\u003c/code\u003e flag for Local server.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf the list is empty, default toolsets will be used. Invalid or unknown toolsets are silently ignored without error and will not prevent the server from starting. Whitespace is ignored.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eX-MCP-Tools\u003c/code\u003e: Comma-separated list of tools to enable. E.g. \"get_file_contents,issue_read,pull_request_read\".\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEquivalent to \u003ccode\u003eGITHUB_TOOLS\u003c/code\u003e env var or \u003ccode\u003e--tools\u003c/code\u003e flag for Local server.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eInvalid tools will throw an error and prevent the server from starting. Whitespace is ignored.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eX-MCP-Readonly\u003c/code\u003e: Enables only \"read\" tools.\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEquivalent to \u003ccode\u003eGITHUB_READ_ONLY\u003c/code\u003e env var for Local server.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf this header is empty, \"false\", \"f\", \"no\", \"n\", \"0\", or \"off\" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eX-MCP-Lockdown\u003c/code\u003e: Enables lockdown mode, hiding public issue details created by users without push access.\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEquivalent to \u003ccode\u003eGITHUB_LOCKDOWN_MODE\u003c/code\u003e env var for Local server.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf this header is empty, \"false\", \"f\", \"no\", \"n\", \"0\", or \"off\" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eX-MCP-Insiders\u003c/code\u003e: Enables insiders mode for early access to new features.\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEquivalent to \u003ccode\u003eGITHUB_INSIDERS\u003c/code\u003e env var or \u003ccode\u003e--insiders\u003c/code\u003e flag for Local server.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf this header is empty, \"false\", \"f\", \"no\", \"n\", \"0\", or \"off\" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLooking for examples?\u003c/strong\u003e See the \u003ca href=\"/github/github-mcp-server/blob/main/docs/server-configuration.md\"\u003eServer Configuration Guide\u003c/a\u003e for common recipes like minimal setups, read-only mode, and combining tools with toolsets.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExample:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Remote GitHub MCP server supports the following URL path patterns:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/\u003c/code\u003e - Default toolset (see \u003ca href=\"/github/github-mcp-server/blob/main/README.md#default-toolset\"\u003e\"default\" toolset\u003c/a\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/readonly\u003c/code\u003e - Default toolset in read-only mode\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/insiders\u003c/code\u003e - Default toolset with insiders mode enabled\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/readonly/insiders\u003c/code\u003e - Default toolset in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/x/all\u003c/code\u003e - All available toolsets\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/x/all/readonly\u003c/code\u003e - All available toolsets in read-only mode\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/x/all/insiders\u003c/code\u003e - All available toolsets with insiders mode enabled\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/x/all/readonly/insiders\u003c/code\u003e - All available toolsets in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/x/{toolset}\u003c/code\u003e - Single specific toolset\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/x/{toolset}/readonly\u003c/code\u003e - Single specific toolset in read-only mode\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/x/{toolset}/insiders\u003c/code\u003e - Single specific toolset with insiders mode enabled\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e/x/{toolset}/readonly/insiders\u003c/code\u003e - Single specific toolset in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eNote: \u003ccode\u003e{toolset}\u003c/code\u003e can only be a single toolset, not a comma-separated list. To combine multiple toolsets, use the \u003ccode\u003eX-MCP-Toolsets\u003c/code\u003e header instead. Path modifiers like \u003ccode\u003e/readonly\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e/insiders\u003c/code\u003e can be combined with the \u003ccode\u003eX-MCP-Insiders\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eX-MCP-Readonly\u003c/code\u003e headers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExample:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate built using this repository as a library, and binding it into GitHub server infrastructure with an internal repository. You can open issues and propose changes in this repository, and we regularly update the remote server to include the latest version of this code.","","The remote server has [additional tools](#toolsets-only-available-in-the-remote-mcp-server) that are not available in the local MCP server, such as the `create_pull_request_with_copilot` tool for invoking Copilot coding agent.","","## Remote MCP Toolsets","","Below is a table of available toolsets for the remote GitHub MCP Server. Each toolset is provided as a distinct URL so you can mix and match to create the perfect combination of tools for your use-case. Add `/readonly` to the end of any URL to restrict the tools in the toolset to only those that enable read access. |","| \u003cpicture\u003e\u003csource media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: dark)\" srcset=\"../pkg/octicons/icons/book-dark.png\"\u003e\u003csource media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: light)\" srcset=\"../pkg/octicons/icons/book-light.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"../pkg/octicons/icons/book-light.png\" width=\"20\" height=\"20\" alt=\"book\"\u003e\u003c/picture\u003e\u003cbr\u003e`github_support_docs_search` | Retrieve documentation to answer GitHub product and support questions. Topics include: GitHub Actions Workflows, Authentication, ... | https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/x/github_support_docs_search | [Install](https://insiders.vscode.dev/redirect/mcp/install?name=gh-github_support_docs_search\u0026config=%7B%22type%22%3A%20%22http%22%2C%22url%22%3A%20%22https%3A%2F%2Fapi.githubcopilot.com%2Fmcp%2Fx%2Fgithub_support_docs_search%22%7D) | [read-only](https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/x/github_support_docs_search/readonly) | [Install read-only](https://insiders.vscode.dev/redirect/mcp/install?name=gh-github_support_docs_search\u0026config=%7B%22type%22%3A%20%22http%22%2C%22url%22%3A%20%22https%3A%2F%2Fapi.githubcopilot.com%2Fmcp%2Fx%2Fgithub_support_docs_search%2Freadonly%22%7D) |","\u003c!-- END AUTOMATED REMOTE TOOLSETS --\u003e","","### Optional Headers","","The Remote GitHub MCP server has optional headers equivalent to the Local server env vars or flags:","","- `X-MCP-Toolsets`: Comma-separated list of toolsets to enable. E.g. \"repos,issues\".","    - Equivalent to `GITHUB_TOOLSETS` env var or `--toolsets` flag for Local server.","    - If the list is empty, default toolsets will be used. Invalid or unknown toolsets are silently ignored without error and will not prevent the server from starting. Whitespace is ignored.","- `X-MCP-Tools`: Comma-separated list of tools to enable. E.g. \"get_file_contents,issue_read,pull_request_read\".","    - Equivalent to `GITHUB_TOOLS` env var or `--tools` flag for Local server.","    - Invalid tools will throw an error and prevent the server from starting. Whitespace is ignored.","- `X-MCP-Readonly`: Enables only \"read\" tools.","    - Equivalent to `GITHUB_READ_ONLY` env var for Local server.","    - If this header is empty, \"false\", \"f\", \"no\", \"n\", \"0\", or \"off\" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.","- `X-MCP-Lockdown`: Enables lockdown mode, hiding public issue details created by users without push access.","    - Equivalent to `GITHUB_LOCKDOWN_MODE` env var for Local server.","    - If this header is empty, \"false\", \"f\", \"no\", \"n\", \"0\", or \"off\" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.","- `X-MCP-Insiders`: Enables insiders mode for early access to new features.","    - Equivalent to `GITHUB_INSIDERS` env var or `--insiders` flag for Local server.","    - If this header is empty, \"false\", \"f\", \"no\", \"n\", \"0\", or \"off\" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.","","\u003e **Looking for examples?** See the [Server Configuration Guide](./server-configuration.md) for common recipes like minimal setups, read-only mode, and combining tools with toolsets.","","Example:","","```json","{","    \"type\": \"http\",","    \"url\": \"https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/\",","    \"headers\": {","        \"X-MCP-Toolsets\": \"repos,issues\",","        \"X-MCP-Readonly\": \"true\",","        \"X-MCP-Lockdown\": \"false\"","    }","}","```","","### Insiders Mode","","The remote GitHub MCP Server offers an insiders version with early access to new features and experimental tools. You can enable insiders mode in two ways:","","1. **Via URL path** - Append `/insiders` to the URL:","","   ```json","   {","       \"type\": \"http\",","       \"url\": \"https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/insiders\"","   }","   ```","","2. **Via header** - Set the `X-MCP-Insiders` header to `true`:","","   ```json","   {","       \"type\": \"http\",","       \"url\": \"https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/\",","       \"headers\": {","           \"X-MCP-Insiders\": \"true\"","       }","   }","   ```","","Both methods can be combined with other path modifiers (like `/readonly`) and headers.","","### URL Path Parameters","","The Remote GitHub MCP server supports the following URL path patterns:","","- `/` - Default toolset (see [\"default\" toolset](../README.md#default-toolset))","- `/readonly` - Default toolset in read-only mode","- `/insiders` - Default toolset with insiders mode enabled","- `/readonly/insiders` - Default toolset in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled","- `/x/all` - All available toolsets","- `/x/all/readonly` - All available toolsets in read-only mode","- `/x/all/insiders` - All available toolsets with insiders mode enabled","- `/x/all/readonly/insiders` - All available toolsets in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled","- `/x/{toolset}` - Single specific toolset","- `/x/{toolset}/readonly` - Single specific toolset in read-only mode","- `/x/{toolset}/insiders` - Single specific toolset with insiders mode enabled","- `/x/{toolset}/readonly/insiders` - Single specific toolset in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled","","Note: `{toolset}` can only be a single toolset, not a comma-separated list. To combine multiple toolsets, use the `X-MCP-Toolsets` header instead. Path modifiers like `/readonly` and `/insiders` can be combined with the `X-MCP-Insiders` or `X-MCP-Readonly` headers.","","Example:","","```json","{","    \"type\": \"http\",","    \"url\": 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://insiders.vscode.dev/redirect/mcp/install?name=github&amp;config=%7B%22type%22%3A%20%22http%22%2C%22url%22%3A%20%22https%3A%2F%2Fapi.githubcopilot.com%2Fmcp%2F%22%7D" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b6a1f2b38f194fcfeef57424328804eb5bc5f3845e07c0fe8559437928d5f792/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f56535f436f64652d496e7374616c6c5f5365727665722d3030393846463f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265266c6f676f3d76697375616c73747564696f636f6465266c6f676f436f6c6f723d7768697465" alt="Install in VS Code" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/VS_Code-Install_Server-0098FF?style=flat-square&amp;logo=visualstudiocode&amp;logoColor=white" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> <a href="https://insiders.vscode.dev/redirect/mcp/install?name=github&amp;config=%7B%22type%22%3A%20%22http%22%2C%22url%22%3A%20%22https%3A%2F%2Fapi.githubcopilot.com%2Fmcp%2F%22%7D&amp;quality=insiders" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/dd44190adf289350f1b0209e6ef30ecf42e019011c54c94df77918149ef6760d/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f56535f436f64655f496e7369646572732d496e7374616c6c5f5365727665722d3234626661353f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265266c6f676f3d76697375616c73747564696f636f6465266c6f676f436f6c6f723d7768697465" alt="Install in VS Code Insiders" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/VS_Code_Insiders-Install_Server-24bfa5?style=flat-square&amp;logo=visualstudiocode&amp;logoColor=white" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Easily connect to the GitHub MCP Server using the hosted version – no local setup or runtime required.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>URL:</strong> <a href="https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/" rel="nofollow">https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">About</h2><a id="user-content-about" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: About" href="#about"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The remote GitHub MCP server is built using this repository as a library, and binding it into GitHub server infrastructure with an internal repository. You can open issues and propose changes in this repository, and we regularly update the remote server to include the latest version of this code.</p>
<p dir="auto">The remote server has <a href="#toolsets-only-available-in-the-remote-mcp-server">additional tools</a> that are not available in the local MCP server, such as the <code>create_pull_request_with_copilot</code> tool for invoking Copilot coding agent.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Remote MCP Toolsets</h2><a id="user-content-remote-mcp-toolsets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Remote MCP Toolsets" href="#remote-mcp-toolsets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Below is a table of available toolsets for the remote GitHub MCP Server. Each toolset is provided as a distinct URL so you can mix and match to create the perfect combination of tools for your use-case. Add <code>/readonly</code> to the end of any URL to restrict the tools in the toolset to only those that enable read access. We also provide the option to use <a href="#headers">headers</a> instead.</p>

<thead>

<th>Name</th>
<th>Description</th>

<th>1-Click Install (VS Code)</th>
<th>Read-only Link</th>
<th>1-Click Read-only Install (VS Code)</th>
</tr>
</thead>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Additional <em>Remote</em> Server Toolsets</h3><a id="user-content-additional-remote-server-toolsets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Additional Remote Server Toolsets" href="#additional-remote-server-toolsets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These toolsets are only available in the remote GitHub MCP Server and are not included in the local MCP server.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Optional Headers</h3><a id="user-content-optional-headers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Optional Headers" href="#optional-headers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Remote GitHub MCP server has optional headers equivalent to the Local server env vars or flags:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>X-MCP-Toolsets</code>: Comma-separated list of toolsets to enable. E.g. "repos,issues".
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Equivalent to <code>GITHUB_TOOLSETS</code> env var or <code>--toolsets</code> flag for Local server.</li>
<li>If the list is empty, default toolsets will be used. Invalid or unknown toolsets are silently ignored without error and will not prevent the server from starting. Whitespace is ignored.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>X-MCP-Tools</code>: Comma-separated list of tools to enable. E.g. "get_file_contents,issue_read,pull_request_read".
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Equivalent to <code>GITHUB_TOOLS</code> env var or <code>--tools</code> flag for Local server.</li>
<li>Invalid tools will throw an error and prevent the server from starting. Whitespace is ignored.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>X-MCP-Readonly</code>: Enables only "read" tools.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Equivalent to <code>GITHUB_READ_ONLY</code> env var for Local server.</li>
<li>If this header is empty, "false", "f", "no", "n", "0", or "off" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>X-MCP-Lockdown</code>: Enables lockdown mode, hiding public issue details created by users without push access.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Equivalent to <code>GITHUB_LOCKDOWN_MODE</code> env var for Local server.</li>
<li>If this header is empty, "false", "f", "no", "n", "0", or "off" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>X-MCP-Insiders</code>: Enables insiders mode for early access to new features.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Equivalent to <code>GITHUB_INSIDERS</code> env var or <code>--insiders</code> flag for Local server.</li>
<li>If this header is empty, "false", "f", "no", "n", "0", or "off" (ignoring whitespace and case), it will be interpreted as false. All other values are interpreted as true.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Looking for examples?</strong> See the <a href="/github/github-mcp-server/blob/main/docs/server-configuration.md">Server Configuration Guide</a> for common recipes like minimal setups, read-only mode, and combining tools with toolsets.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;http&quot;,
    &quot;url&quot;: &quot;https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/&quot;,
    &quot;headers&quot;: {
        &quot;X-MCP-Toolsets&quot;: &quot;repos,issues&quot;,
        &quot;X-MCP-Readonly&quot;: &quot;true&quot;,
        &quot;X-MCP-Lockdown&quot;: &quot;false&quot;
    }
}"><pre>{
    <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"url"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"headers"</span>: {
        <span class="pl-ent">"X-MCP-Toolsets"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>repos,issues<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        <span class="pl-ent">"X-MCP-Readonly"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        <span class="pl-ent">"X-MCP-Lockdown"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>false<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    }
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Insiders Mode</h3><a id="user-content-insiders-mode" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Insiders Mode" href="#insiders-mode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The remote GitHub MCP Server offers an insiders version with early access to new features and experimental tools. You can enable insiders mode in two ways:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Via URL path</strong> - Append <code>/insiders</code> to the URL:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;http&quot;,
    &quot;url&quot;: &quot;https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/insiders&quot;
}"><pre>{
    <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"url"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/insiders<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Via header</strong> - Set the <code>X-MCP-Insiders</code> header to <code>true</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;http&quot;,
    &quot;url&quot;: &quot;https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/&quot;,
    &quot;headers&quot;: {
        &quot;X-MCP-Insiders&quot;: &quot;true&quot;
    }
}"><pre>{
    <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"url"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"headers"</span>: {
        <span class="pl-ent">"X-MCP-Insiders"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    }
}</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Both methods can be combined with other path modifiers (like <code>/readonly</code>) and headers.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">URL Path Parameters</h3><a id="user-content-url-path-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: URL Path Parameters" href="#url-path-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Remote GitHub MCP server supports the following URL path patterns:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>/</code> - Default toolset (see <a href="/github/github-mcp-server/blob/main/README.md#default-toolset">"default" toolset</a>)</li>
<li><code>/readonly</code> - Default toolset in read-only mode</li>
<li><code>/insiders</code> - Default toolset with insiders mode enabled</li>
<li><code>/readonly/insiders</code> - Default toolset in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled</li>
<li><code>/x/all</code> - All available toolsets</li>
<li><code>/x/all/readonly</code> - All available toolsets in read-only mode</li>
<li><code>/x/all/insiders</code> - All available toolsets with insiders mode enabled</li>
<li><code>/x/all/readonly/insiders</code> - All available toolsets in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled</li>
<li><code>/x/{toolset}</code> - Single specific toolset</li>
<li><code>/x/{toolset}/readonly</code> - Single specific toolset in read-only mode</li>
<li><code>/x/{toolset}/insiders</code> - Single specific toolset with insiders mode enabled</li>
<li><code>/x/{toolset}/readonly/insiders</code> - Single specific toolset in read-only mode with insiders mode enabled</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Note: <code>{toolset}</code> can only be a single toolset, not a comma-separated list. To combine multiple toolsets, use the <code>X-MCP-Toolsets</code> header instead. Path modifiers like <code>/readonly</code> and <code>/insiders</code> can be combined with the <code>X-MCP-Insiders</code> or <code>X-MCP-Readonly</code> headers.</p>
<p dir="auto">Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;http&quot;,
    &quot;url&quot;: &quot;https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/x/issues/readonly&quot;
}"><pre>{
    <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"url"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://api.githubcopilot.com/mcp/x/issues/readonly<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
</article></div><div class="d-none"></div></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><div class="d-none"></div></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> <script type="application/json" id="__PRIMER_DATA__R_1___">{"resolvedServerColorMode":"day"}</script></div>
</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>

  </div>
